Implicit arguments need to be supplied when they are
not fixed by the given arguments.

## Reflexive and transitive closure

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10359" class="Keyword">infix</a>  <a id="10366" class="Number">2</a> <a id="10368" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/Extensions.md %}{% raw %}#10421" class="Datatype Operator">_⟶*_</a>
<a id="10373" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="10379" class="Number">1</a> <a id="10381" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/Extensions.md %}{% raw %}#10625" class="Function Operator">begin_</a>

As a corollary, terms that reduce are not values.

## Normalise
